      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="List_of_lunar_eclipses_between_-499_and_-400">
        List of lunar eclipses between -499 and -400
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_5th-century_BCE_lunar_eclipses&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: List of lunar eclipses between -499 and -400">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       There were 242
       <a href="/wiki/Lunar_eclipse" title="Lunar eclipse">
        lunar eclipse
       </a>
       events between -499 and -400 (500 BCE to 401 BCE)
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>

             <img alt="Commons page" data-file-height="1376" data-file-width="1024" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/12px-Commons-logo.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/18px-Commons-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/24px-Commons-logo.svg.png 2x" title="Commons page" width="12"/>
             <a class="extiw" href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:Lunar_eclipse" title="commons:Category:Lunar eclipse">
              Commons
             </a>
            </li>
            <li>
             <img alt="Portal" data-file-height="28" data-file-width="32" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fd/Portal-puzzle.svg/16px-Portal-puzzle.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fd/Portal-puzzle.svg/24px-Portal-puzzle.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fd/Portal-puzzle.svg/32px-Portal-puzzle.svg.png 2x" title="Portal" width="16"/>
             <a href="/wiki/Portal:Moon" title="Portal:Moon">
              Portal
             </a>
            </li>
            <li>
             <img alt="WikiProject" data-file-height="100" data-file-width="100" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/People_icon.svg/16px-People_icon.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/People_icon.svg/24px-People_icon.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/People_icon.svg/32px-People_icon.svg.png 2x" title="WikiProject" width="16"/>
             <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Eclipses" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Eclipses">
              WikiProject
             </a>
            </li>
            <li>
             <span style="background-color: #FC6">
              →
             </span>
             <small>
              symbol denotes next eclipse in series
             </small>
            </li>
           </ul>
          </div>
         </td>
        </tr>
       </table>
